Beginner's Basics

Show/hide all levels
Active Irena's Wind Piercing
Master Level 5
Description Summons Irena to inflicts significant damage to multiple monsters with a single powerful blow. Skill level can be increased depending on your level.
Level 1 MP Cost: 15, Damage: 530%, Max Enemies Penetrated: 4
5 MP Cost: 27, Damage: 750%, Max Enemies Penetrated: 6
Active Irena's Wind Piercing
Master Level 5
Description Summons Irena to inflicts significant damage to multiple monsters with a single powerful blow. Skill level can be increased depending on your level.

5 MP Cost: 27, Damage: 750%, Max Enemies Penetrated: 6
Show/hide all levels
Active Irena's Wind
Master Level 10
Description Summons a spirit that automatically performs an area attack on the enemies you are fighting. Skill level increases by 1 every 15 levels.
Level 1 MP Cost: 11, Damage: 70%, Duration: 110 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.
10 MP Cost: 20, Damage: 160%, Duration: 200 sec
The damage of Ultimate Explorer minion skills is calculated differently from that of the character.

Show/hide all levels
Passive Adventurer's Curiosity
Master Level 6
Description Your curiosity and attention to detail grants you bonuses to Critical Rate and the chance of adding monsters to your Monster Collection.
This bonus is multiplicative rather than additive.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Bowman job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +10%, Critical Rate: +3%
6 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +35%, Critical Rate: +10%
Passive Adventurer's Curiosity
Master Level 6
Description Your curiosity and attention to detail grants you bonuses to Critical Rate and the chance of adding monsters to your Monster Collection.
This bonus is multiplicative rather than additive.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 3 times, once for each unique Explorer Bowman job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +10%, Critical Rate: +3%
2 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +15%, Critical Rate: +4%
3 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +20%, Critical Rate: +6%
4 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +25%, Critical Rate: +7%
5 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +30%, Critical Rate: +9%
6 Chance to add monsters to Monster Collection: +35%, Critical Rate: +10%

Show/hide all levels
Active Double Jump
Master Level 10
Description Allows you to use the Double Jump skill to move very quickly. Double-tap the up arrow key to jump again while in mid-air. Double-tap the down arrow key to descend more quickly. If you use Action Customization, you can move up in the air with the up arrow and jump keys, and descend with the down arrow and jump keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF.
Level 1 MP Cost: 28, allows you to jump a greater distance
10 MP Cost: 10, allows you to jump a greater distance

Crossbowman Guide

Show/hide all levels
Active Piercing Arrow
Master Level 20
Description Fire a piercing arrow. Its effect increases with each enemy it hits.
Unlocks Empowered Arrows at Level 20.
Unlocks Piercing II at Level 20.
Level 1 MP Cost: 24, Damage: 92%, Max Enemies Pierced: 6, Number of Attacks: 4.
Final damage increases by 15% with each enemy pierced, and damage is doubled.
20 MP Cost: 36, Damage: 130%, Max Enemies Pierced: 6, Number of Attacks: 4.
Final damage increases by 15% with each enemy pierced, and damage is doubled.

Active Covering Fire
Master Level 9
Description Fire arrows while leaping backwards. While firing, you'll have 100% Knockback Resistance. If you press and hold the skill key, you will fire arrows rapidly while in mid-air. You will temporarily not be pushed back by any attack after casting.
Level 1 MP Cost: 3, if you press and hold the skill key after jumping a certain distance backward, you will attack enemies at up to 81% of damage for 2 sec while in mid-air
9 MP Cost: 5, if you press and hold the skill key after jumping a certain distance backward, you will attack enemies at up to 105% of damage for 2 sec while in mid-air
Active Covering Fire
Master Level 9
Description Fire arrows while leaping backwards. While firing, you'll have 100% Knockback Resistance. If you press and hold the skill key, you will fire arrows rapidly while in mid-air. You will temporarily not be pushed back by any attack after casting.

Passive Soul Arrow: Crossbow
Master Level 20
Description Allows you to fire your crossbow without consuming arrows and increases Attack Power.
The crossbow arrows in your inventory with the highest Attack Power will be used to calculate damage.
Level 1 Attack Power +11. Allows you to attack without consuming arrows.
20 Attack Power +30. Allows you to attack without consuming arrows.

Passive Final Attack : Crossbow
Master Level 20
Description Chance to deal additional hits after a direct attack. Must have a crossbow equipped.
Required Skill: Crossbow Mastery Lv. 3
Level 1 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 2% chance to deal a final attack that deals 100% damage.
20 [Final Attack Skill] Has a 40% chance to deal a final attack that deals 150% damage.

Sniper's Scope

Show/hide all levels
Passive Empowered Arrows
Master Level 10
Description Empowers certain attack skills as you use them. Enhances Piercing Arrow (Piercing Arrow II is unaffected).
Unlocks Greater Empowered Arrows at Level 10.
Required Skill: Piercing Arrow Lv. 20
Level 1 After striking enemies with Piercing Arrow 3 times, your next Piercing Arrow will be upgraded to an Empowered Piercing Arrow.
Empowered Piercing Arrow - MP Cost: 30, Damage: 203%, Max Enemies Pierced: 8, Number of Attacks: 6
[Passive Effects - Piercing Arrow Damage: +104% points]
10 After striking enemies with Piercing Arrow 3 times, your next Piercing Arrow will be upgraded to an Empowered Piercing Arrow.
Empowered Piercing Arrow - MP Cost: 30, Damage: 230%, Max Enemies Pierced: 8, Number of Attacks: 6
[Passive Effects - Piercing Arrow Damage: +140% points]

Arrow Fragment bounces off the first enemy hit, dealing 360% damage 4 times on up to 2 enemies.

Passive Greater Empowered Arrows
Master Level 20
Description Enhances the strength of your Empowered Arrows.
Empowered Piercing Arrow is enhanced to Empowered Piercing Arrow II, and Empowered Arrows can also be used during Snipe.
Striking an enemy with Empowered skills grants you the Marked Target buff, which is unaffected by duration increases. Permanently increases Final Damage and Ignore Defense.
Required Skill: Empowered Arrows Lv. 10
Level 1 When Piercing Arrow hits 3 times, Empowered Piercing Arrow II can be activated.
When Snipe hits 3 times, Empowered Snipe can be activated.
Empowered Piercing Arrow II: MP Cost: 87. Pierces up to 10 enemies, dealing 351% damage 6 times. Explodes at end trajectory, dealing 242% damage 10 times to up to 10 enemies. Empowered Snipe: MP Cost: 105. Deals 402% damage 10 times with +7% Ignore DEF and +100% Critical Rate. Striking an enemy marked by Snipe deals 225% additional damage 10 times. Marked Target: Final Damage +4% for 30 sec, Ignore Monster DEF: +13%. [Passive Effect] Final Damage +8%, Ignore DEF: +20%.
20 When Piercing Arrow hits 3 times, Empowered Piercing Arrow II can be activated.
When Snipe hits 3 times, Empowered Snipe can be activated.

Marked Target: Final Damage +4% for 30 sec, Ignore Monster DEF: +13%. [Passive Effect] Final Damage +8%, Ignore DEF: +20%.

Active Arrow Illusion
Master Level 30
Description Summons an arrow illusion for a short time to draw enemies in and damage them. If you get hit during the skill, you will launch a powerful counterattack. Not affected by attack reflection. Also increases Ignore Defense permanently.
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, summon Arrow Illusion with 27500 HP for 30 sec
Arrow Illusion periodically deals 113% damage and pulls in enemies. 12% chance to stun hit enemies for 1 sec.
When Arrow Illusion takes damage, reflect 330% of damage.
[Passive Effects - Ignore Defense: 1%]
30 MP Cost: 70, summon Arrow Illusion with 100000 HP for 30 sec
Arrow Illusion periodically deals 200% damage and pulls in enemies. 70% chance to stun hit enemies for 4 sec.
When Arrow Illusion takes damage, reflect 1200% of damage.
[Passive Effects - Ignore Defense: 30%]
31 MP Cost: 70, summon Arrow Illusion with 102500 HP for 30 sec
Arrow Illusion periodically deals 203% damage and pulls in enemies. 72% chance to stun hit enemies for 4 sec.

[Passive Effects - Ignore Defense: 31%]

Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]
25 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 55 sec, restores 30% HP when used, able to use 17 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +5]
30 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 60 sec, restores 35% HP when used, able to use 20 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +6]

Master Level 25
Description The collapsing space between the Mirror World and reality become linked with Will's Erda, causing the spider within the mirror to temporarily materialize in reality.

Spatial Collapse - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 468%, Number of Attacks: 15, Once complete, summons True Arachnid Reflection.
True Arachnid Reflection - Duration: 50 sec, Goes into attack mode at set intervals. During attack mode, uses spider legs 10 times to deal 182% damage 8 times. If the spider legs attack one target 5 consecutive times, attack mode will end immediately. 3 sec cooldown after attack mode ends.
Cooldown: 250 sec

Cooldown: 60 sec.

Active Split Shot
Master Level 25
Description Magically enchants your arrows to explode as they approach the enemy, releasing countless more arrows. Arrow Fragments activated by Piercing Arrow don't split.
Level 1 MP Cost: 800, Duration: 72 sec. Landing a hit with Full Burst Shot after using Piercing Arrow, Snipe, Empowered Piercing Arrow, Empowered Snipe, Ultimate Piercing, Ultimate Snipe, Final Aim, or Repeating Crossbow Cartridge causes your arrow to split and attack up to 10 enemies, dealing 728% damage 5 times.
Ignore Defense: 25%

Active Surge Bolt
Master Level 25
Description Concentrate and deploy a powerful spirit arrow.
Concentrate by pressing the key down. Activates an enhanced Surge Bolt when used after concentration is complete. Using a different skill while you concentrate will not cancel this skill.
You can activate the Surge Bolt while using Full Burst Shot after using Snipe, Piercing, High Speed Shot, and Repeating Crossbow Cartridge, if you've concentrated for just a short time. However, you need to use up all of your arrows to use Full Burst Shot.
Also, if this skill hits the enemy, obtain the Marked Target buff.
The Final Attack will not be applied to the Surge Bolt.
Level 1 MP Cost: 750, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 598%, Number of Attacks: 12, Number of Hit Attacks: 2. Makes 2 attacks for 884% damage after concentration is complete
Additional Monster DEF Ignored: 50%, Additional Critical Rate: +100%
Max Concentration Duration: 10 sec
Cooldown: 20 sec
25 MP Cost: 750, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 1150%, Number of Attacks: 12, Number of Hit Attacks: 2. Makes 2 attacks for 1700% damage after concentration is complete
Additional Monster DEF Ignored: 50%, Additional Critical Rate: +100%
Max Concentration Duration: 10 sec
Cooldown: 20 sec
30 MP Cost: 750, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 1265%, Number of Attacks: 12, Number of Hit Attacks: 2. Makes 2 attacks for 1870% damage after concentration is complete
Additional Monster DEF Ignored: 50%, Additional Critical Rate: +100%
Max Concentration Duration: 10 sec
Cooldown: 20 sec

Active Repeating Crossbow Cartridge
Master Level 25
Description Use a special cartridge that allows you to fire multiple arrows at once. Use the skill again to activate a Full Burst Shot with the same cartridge. Full Burst Shot is attracted to the targeted enemy within range and attacks the boss with the highest HP first. Successful hits with Full Burst Shot grannts the Marked Target buff.
Level 1 MP Cost: 750, Duration: 60 sec, Usable Cartridges: 8
Full Burst Shot: MP Cost: 150, Cartridge Used: 1, Damage: 520%, Number of Arrow Attacks: 9, Arrows Fired: 4, DEF Ignored: 25%, Critical Rate: 100%
Cooldown: 120 sec

Active Sol Janus: Dawn
Master Level 30
Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Mastery Skills

Mastery Skills are affected by Hyper Skill passives (if applicable) and Boost Node enhancements applied to the base skill.

Show/hide all levels
Active HEXA Snipe
Master Level 30
Description Fires a carefully-aimed shot to deal severe damage.
Also, Empowered Arrows for Snipe are enhanced. Striking an enemy with Snipe prepares the second Snipe with Empowered Arrows and the fourth Snipe with 2 more special Ultimate Arrows.
When Snipe hits, the enemy's weaknesses are analyzed then marked. When attacking a marked enemy with Empowered Arrows, the enemy's weakness is exploited to fire an additional attack.
Snipe and Snipe enhanced with Empowered Arrows target the enemy with the highest Max HP first.
Require Skills: Snipe Lv. 30, Greater Empowered Arrows Lv. 20
Level 1 #Snipe# - MP Cost: 60, Damage: 496%, Number of Attacks: 9
Enemies struck are marked.
Empowered Snipe - MP Cost: 120, Damage: 490%, Number of Attacks: 10
When striking a marked enemy, Damage: 323%, Number of Additional Attacks: 5
Ultimate Snipe - MP Cost: 120
Damage: 258%, Number of Attacks: 10, Number of Arrows: 2
When striking a marked enemy, Damage: 323%, Number of Additional Attacks: 5
Snipe, Empowered Snipe, and Ultimate Snipe - Ignore Defense: 30%, Bonus Critical Rate: 100%
30 #Snipe# - MP Cost: 70, Damage: 670%, Number of Attacks: 9
Enemies struck are marked.
Empowered Snipe - MP Cost: 140, Damage: 635%, Number of Attacks: 10
When striking a marked enemy, Damage: 410%, Number of Additional Attacks: 5
Ultimate Snipe - MP Cost: 140
Damage: 345%, Number of Attacks: 10, Number of Arrows: 2
When striking a marked enemy, Damage: 410%, Number of Additional Attacks: 5
Snipe, Empowered Snipe, and Ultimate Snipe - Ignore Defense: 40%, Bonus Critical Rate: 100%

Active HEXA Piercing Arrow
Master Level 30
Description Fires an arrow. Its effect increases with each enemy it hits.
Empowered Arrows is enhanced further. After landing a Piercing Arrow, the second Piercing Arrow will be upgraded to an Empowered Piercing Arrow, and the fourth Piercing Arrow will become an Ultimate Arrow
Upon striking their first foe, your Piercing Arrow skill now fragments, dealing damage to additional enemies.
Permanently enhances HEXA Snipe.
Required Skill: Piercing Arrow II Lv. 30, Greater Empowered Arrows Lv. 20
Level 1 Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 55, Max Enemies Penetrated: 8, Damage: 381%, Number of Attacks: 5
Final Damage for Each Enemy Penetrated: +15% (increase occurs between hits )
Arrow Fragments bounce off the first enemy penetrated, dealing 392% damage 4 times to up to 3 enemies
Empowered Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 467%, Number of Attacks: 10
Ultimate Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 477%, Number of Attacks: 6. The arrow explodes at the point where it disappears, dealing 324% damage, 10 times, to up to 10 enemies.
[Passive Effect: HEXA Snipe Damage: +2%p, HEXA Empowered Snipe: +4%p, Bonus HEXA Empowered Snipe Damage: +2%p, HEXA Ultimate Snipe: +2%p, Bonus HEXA Ultimate Snipe Damage: +2%p]
30 Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 65, Max Enemies Penetrated: 8, Damage: 555%, Number of Attacks: 5
Final Damage for Each Enemy Penetrated: +15% (increase occurs between hits )
Arrow Fragments bounce off the first enemy penetrated, dealing 595% damage 4 times to up to 3 enemies
Empowered Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 110, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 670%, Number of Attacks: 10
Ultimate Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 110, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 680%, Number of Attacks: 6. The arrow explodes at the point where it disappears, dealing 440% damage, 10 times, to up to 10 enemies.
[Passive Effect: HEXA Snipe Damage: +60%p, HEXA Empowered Snipe: +120%p, Bonus HEXA Empowered Snipe Damage: +60%p, HEXA Ultimate Snipe: +60%p, Bonus HEXA Ultimate Snipe Damage: +60%p]
Active HEXA Piercing Arrow
Master Level 30
Description Fires an arrow. Its effect increases with each enemy it hits.
Empowered Arrows is enhanced further. After landing a Piercing Arrow, the second Piercing Arrow will be upgraded to an Empowered Piercing Arrow, and the fourth Piercing Arrow will become an Ultimate Arrow
Upon striking their first foe, your Piercing Arrow skill now fragments, dealing damage to additional enemies.
Permanently enhances HEXA Snipe.
Required Skill: Piercing Arrow II Lv. 30, Greater Empowered Arrows Lv. 20
Level 1 Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 55, Max Enemies Penetrated: 8, Damage: 381%, Number of Attacks: 5
Final Damage for Each Enemy Penetrated: +15% (increase occurs between hits )
Arrow Fragments bounce off the first enemy penetrated, dealing 392% damage 4 times to up to 3 enemies
Empowered Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 467%, Number of Attacks: 10
Ultimate Piercing Arrow: MP Cost: 100, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 477%, Number of Attacks: 6. The arrow explodes at the point where it disappears, dealing 324% damage, 10 times, to up to 10 enemies.
[Passive Effect: HEXA Snipe Damage: +2%p, HEXA Empowered Snipe: +4%p, Bonus HEXA Empowered Snipe Damage: +2%p, HEXA Ultimate Snipe: +2%p, Bonus HEXA Ultimate Snipe Damage: +2%p]

Enhancements

Enhancements require the corresponding V Skill to be leveled to max and equipped. Final Damage bonuses from Enhancements increase linearly each level, with a jump at levels 10, 20, and 30.
